         <script type="text/javascript">
          /* <![CDATA[ */
 	jQuery(document).ready(function($){
 		$('.mobile-nav-toggler-open').on('click',function(){
 			var documentHeight = $(document).height();
 			$('.mobile-nav-toggler-close').show();
 			$(this).hide();
 			$('.page').css({"position":"relative","left":"200px"});
 			$('.mobilenav.mobile-nav-primary').show();
 			$('.mobilenav.mobile-nav-primary').css({
 				"top":"0",
 				"height" : documentHeight,
 			});
 			$('.mobilenav.mobile-nav-primary').insertAfter('.wrapper');
 			var nav_offset = $('.page').offset().left;
 			$('.mobilenav.mobile-nav-primary').css("width",nav_offset);
 			$('.blackbox-sidenav').insertAfter('.wrapper');
 			$('.blackbox-sidenav').css({"display":"inherit","left":"200px"});
 		});
 		$('.blackbox-sidenav').on('click',function(){
 			$('.page').css("left","auto");
 			$('.mobile-nav-toggler-open').show();
 			$('.mobilenav.mobile-nav-primary').hide();
 			$(this).hide();
 		});
 		$('.cat-toggler').on('click',function(){
 			$('.sub').hide();
 			$(this).next('ul').toggle();
 			$('.cat-toggler').removeClass('up');
 			$(this).addClass('up');
 		});
 	});
 /* ]]> */
         </script>

     <script>
      jQuery(document).ready(function($){
 	  var homepage_slider = $('#homepageslider').bxSlider({
 		  mode: 'fade',
 		  auto: true,
 		  adaptiveHeight: true,
 		  onSliderLoad: function(){
 				getSLiderPagerWidth();
 		  },
 		  onSliderResize  : function(){
 			homepage_slider.redrawSlider();
 			getSLiderPagerWidth();
 		},
 	  });
 	  
 	  function getSLiderPagerWidth () {
 		  
 		  var thisSlider = $('#homepageslider-container');
 		  
 		  var numberOfSlides =   thisSlider.find('.bx-wrapper .bx-pager.bx-default-pager a').length;
 		
 		  var bxViewportWidth = thisSlider.find('.bx-viewport').width();
 
 		  var pagerTargetWidth =  bxViewportWidth / numberOfSlides;
 			
 		  $('#homepageslider-container .bx-wrapper .bx-pager.bx-default-pager a').css('width',pagerTargetWidth);
 		  
 	  }
 	  
 	  
 });
     </script>

      jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
 
 		var homepageblocks_slider_initialized = false;
 
 		if ($(document).isBreakpoint('xs')) {
 
 			var homepageblocks_slider = $('#homepageblocks-top').bxSlider({
 				controls : false,
 				onSliderLoad : function() {
 					homepageblocks_slider_initialized = true;
 				},
 				onSliderResize : function() {
 					if (!$(document).isBreakpoint('xs')) {
 						homepageblocks_slider.destroySlider();
 						homepageblocks_slider_initialized = false;
 					}
 				}
 			});
 
 		}
 
 		$(window).resize(function() {
 			if ($(document).isBreakpoint('xs') && !homepageblocks_slider_initialized) {
 
 				var homepageblocks_slider = $('#homepageblocks-top').bxSlider({
 					controls : false,
 					onSliderLoad : function() {
 						homepageblocks_slider_initialized = true;
 					},
 					onSliderResize : function() {
 						if (!$(document).isBreakpoint('xs')) {
 							homepageblocks_slider.destroySlider();
 							homepageblocks_slider_initialized = false;
 						}
 					}
 				});
 
 			}
 		});
 
 	});

     <script>
      jQuery(document).ready(function($){
 
 	var thisBrandSliderContainer = $('#brandstores-list');
 
 	if($(document).isBreakpoint('xs')) {
 		var slide_width = $('#brandstores-list').width();
 	}else{
 		var slide_width = $('#brandstores-list').width() / 3;
 	}
 
 
 	var brandstore_slider = $('.brandstore-slides').bxSlider({
 		minSlides: $(document).isBreakpoint('xs') ? 1 : 3,
 		maxSlides: 3,
 		slideWidth: slide_width,
 		slideMargin: 30,
 		pager: false,
 		infiniteLoop: false,
 		onSliderLoad  : function(){
 			thisBrandSliderContainer.find('.bx-controls').appendTo(thisBrandSliderContainer.find('.product-pager'));
 		},
 		onSliderResize  : function(){
 			resizeTasks();
 		},
 	});
 
 
 	function resizeTasks (elem){
 		if($(document).isBreakpoint('xs')) {
 			brandstore_slider.reloadSlider({
 				minSlides: 1,
 				maxSlides: 1,
 				pager: false,
 				slideWidth: 0,
 				slideMargin: 0,
 				infiniteLoop: false,
 				onSliderLoad  : function(){
 					thisBrandSliderContainer.find('.bx-controls').appendTo(thisBrandSliderContainer.find('.product-pager'));
 				},
 				onSliderResize  : function(){
 					resizeTasks();
 				},
 			});
 		}else{
 			slide_width = $('#brandstores-list').width() / 3;
 			brandstore_slider.reloadSlider({
 				minSlides: 3,
 				maxSlides: 3,
 				slideMargin: 30,
 				pager: false,
 				infiniteLoop: false,
 				slideWidth: slide_width,
 				onSliderLoad  : function(){
 					thisBrandSliderContainer.find('.bx-controls').appendTo(thisBrandSliderContainer.find('.product-pager'));
 				},
 				onSliderResize  : function(){
 					resizeTasks();
 				},
 			});
 		}
 	}
 
 });
     </script>

     	function initialize(latitude,longitude,target) {
     		for (i = 0; i < locations.length; i++) {
     			if(locations[i]['id'] == null)continue;
     			if(locations[i]['type'] == 1){
     	  			var icon 	= '/media/icon_stores_red.svg';
     	  		}else{
     	  			var icon 	= '/media/icon_stores.svg';
     	  		}
     			markers[i]		= [locations[i]['id'],locations[i]['name'],locations[i]['latitude'],locations[i]['longitude'],locations[i]['type'],icon];
     		}
     		var mapProp = {
     	    	center				: new google.maps.LatLng(latitude,longitude),
     	    	zoom				: 7,
     	    	panControl			: true,
     	    	zoomControl			: true,
     	    	zoomControlOptions: {
             		position: google.maps.ControlPosition.LEFT_CENTER
         		},
     	    	scaleControl		: true,
     	    	mapTypeControl		: true,
     	    	streetViewControl	: true,
     			overviewMapControl	: true,
     			rotateControl		: true,
     			scrollwheel			: isMobile()?false:true,
     		    navigationControl	: false,
     		    mapTypeControl		: false,
     		    scaleControl		: false,
     		    draggable			: true,
     	    	mapTypeId			: google.maps.MapTypeId.ROADMAP
     	  	};
     	  	if(typeof target === "undefined" || target === null) {
     	  		var map		= new google.maps.Map(document.getElementById("stores"),mapProp);
     	  	} else {
     	  		var map		= new google.maps.Map(document.getElementById(target),mapProp);
     	  	}
     	  	var styles 	= [
     		  {
     		    featureType: "all",
     		    stylers: [
     		      {saturation: -100},
     		      {lightness: 40},
     		    ]
     		  },{
     		    featureType: "road.arterial",
     		    elementType: "geometry",
     		    stylers: [
     		      { hue: "#00ffee" },
     		      { saturation: 50 }
     		    ]
     		  },{
     		    featureType: "poi.business",
     		    elementType: "labels",
     		    stylers: [
     		      { visibility: "off" }
     		    ]
     		  }
     		];
 
     		map.setOptions({styles: styles});
     	  	var marker, i;
 
     	  	marker 	= new google.maps.Marker({
     	    		position	: new google.maps.LatLng($('input[name="current_position_lat"]').val(),$('input[name="current_position_lng"]').val()),
     	    		icon		: '/media/icon_stores_home.svg',
     				map			: map,
     				clickable	: false
     		});
 
     	  	for (i = 0; i < markers.length; i++) {
     	  		addMarker(markers[i],map,showPin);
     	   	}
 
     	   	var showPin	= [];
     	   	$('.filterCat').each( function(){
     			if(!$(this).hasClass('active')) {
     				var type	= $(this).data('category');
     				if(type == 1) {
     					type = 2;
     				} else {
     					type = 1;
     				}
     				filterMarkers(type);
     			}
     		});
 
     	   	google.maps.event.addListenerOnce(map, 'idle', function(){
     	   		$('#storeInfo').hide();
     			$('.loader').addClass('hide');
     	   	});
     	   	google.maps.event.addListener(map, 'drag', function(){
     	   		$('#storeInfo').hide();
     	   		$('.store').removeClass('active');
     	   	});
     	   	google.maps.event.addListener(map, 'zoom_changed', function(){
     	   		$('#storeInfo').hide();
     	   		$('.store').removeClass('active');
     	   	});
     	   	google.maps.event.addListener(map, 'click', function(){
     	   		$('#storeInfo').hide();
     	   		$('.store').removeClass('active');
     	   	});
     	   	google.maps.event.addListener(map, 'dblclick', function(){
     	   		$('#storeInfo').hide();
     	   		$('.store').removeClass('active');
     	   	});
     	   	google.maps.event.addListener(map, 'maptypeid_changed', function(){
     	   		$('#storeInfo').hide();
     	   		$('.store').removeClass('active');
     	   	});
     	   	saveMap(map);
     	   	return map;
     	}
 
     	filterMarkers = function (category) {
     	    for (i = 0; i < gmarkers.length; i++) {
     	        marker = gmarkers[i];
     	        if (marker.category == category || category == 0 || category.length === 0) {
     	            marker.setVisible(true);
     	        }
     	        else {
     	            marker.setVisible(false);
     	        }
     	    }
     	    if(category == 3) {
     	    	$('.store').addClass('hide');
     	    } else {
     	    	if(category == 0) {
     	    		$('.store').removeClass('hide');
     	    	} else {
     	    		$('.store').each( function(){
     		    		if($(this).data('category') == category) {
     		    			$(this).removeClass('hide');
     		    		} else {
     		    			$(this).addClass('hide');
     		    		}
     		    	});
     	    	}
     	    }
 
     	    return true;
     	}
 
     	function addMarker(marker,map,showPin) {
         	marker 		= new google.maps.Marker({
         		position	: new google.maps.LatLng(marker[2], marker[3]),
         		icon		: marker[5],
         		title		: marker[1],
     			map			: map,
     			store		: marker[0],
     			category	: marker[4],
     		});
     		gmarkers.push(marker);
     		google.maps.event.addListener(marker, 'click', function () {
     			var storeId	= this.get('store');
     	   		$('#storeInfo').hide();
     	   		map.panTo(new google.maps.LatLng((this.getPosition().lat()+1.5),(this.getPosition().lng())));
     	   		map.setZoom(7);
     			showStore(storeId);
     			$('#storeInfo').show();
     			$('.store').each( function(){
     				if($(this).data('storeid') == storeId) {
     					$(this).addClass('active');
     				}
     			});
           	});
     	}
 
     	function saveMap(map) {
     		storeMap	= map;
     	}
 
     	var latitude	= 48.1492;
     	var longitude	= 11.5328;
 
     	function showStore(id){
     		$("html, body").animate({
     			scrollTop: 0
     		}, 500);
     		var storeId		= id;
     		var load		= true;
     		$('.overview .panel-content').each(function( index ) {
     			if(!$(this).hasClass('hide')){
     				$(this).parent('.panel').find('.toggler').trigger('click');
     			}
     		});
     		$('.overview .panel').each(function( index ) {
       			if($(this).attr('id') == 'store-'+storeId){
       				$(this).find('.toggler').trigger('click');
       				load	= false;
       			}
     		});
     		if(load === true){
     			var current_lat	= $('input[name="current_position_lat"]').val();
     			var current_lng	= $('input[name="current_position_lng"]').val();
     			var data		= {store:storeId,lat:current_lat,lng:current_lng};
     			$.get('/stores/store/show/storeId/'+storeId+'/lat/'+current_lat+'/lng/'+current_lng, function(data) {
     				$('#storeInfo').html($(data).find('#ajaxLoad').html());
     			});
     		}
     	}
 
     	$(document).on('click', '#storeInfoClose', function(event) {
     		$('#storeInfo').hide();
     	});
 
     	$(document).on('click', '.store', function(event) {
     		$('.store').removeClass('active');
     		var storeId	= $(this).data('storeid');
     		gmarkers.each( function(store){
     			if(store.get('store') == storeId) {
     				$('#storeInfo').hide();
     		   		storeMap.panTo(new google.maps.LatLng((store.getPosition().lat()+1),(store.getPosition().lng())));
     		   		storeMap.setZoom(7);
     				showStore(store.get('store'));
     				$('#storeInfo').show();
     			}
     		});
     		$(this).addClass('active');
     	});
 
     	$(document).on('click', '.filterCat', function(event) {
     		$(this).toggleClass('active');
     		var category	= $(this).data('category');
     		var active		= $(this).hasClass('active');
     		var categories	= 0;
     		$('.filterCat').each(function() {
     			if($(this).hasClass('active')) {
     				categories++;
     			}
     		});
     		if(categories == 1) {
     			if(true == active && category == 1) {
     				filterMarkers(1);
     			}
     			if(true == active && category == 2) {
     				filterMarkers(2);
     			}
     			if(false == active && category == 1) {
     				filterMarkers(2);
     			}
     			if(false == active && category == 2) {
     				filterMarkers(1);
     			}
     		}
     		if(categories == 2) {
     			filterMarkers(0);
     			return true;
     		}
     		if(categories == 0) {
     			filterMarkers(3);
     			return true;
     		}
     	});
 
     	$(document).on('submit', '#searchStore', function(event) {
     		$('#storeInfo').hide();
       		event.preventDefault();
       		var searchTerm	= $('#searchStore input[name="store"]').val();
       		if($.trim(searchTerm) == '') {
       			$('#searchStore input[name="store"]').focus();
       			return false;
       		}
       		$('#storesModal').modal('show');
     	});
 
     	$(document).on('submit', '#storeSearch', function(event) {
     		$('#storeInfo').hide();
       		event.preventDefault();
       		var searchTerm	= $('#storeSearch input[name="store"]').val();
       		if($.trim(searchTerm) == '') {
       			$('#storeSearch input[name="store"]').focus();
       			return false;
       		}
       		$('#storeSearch button[type="submit"]').focus();
       		loadStores(searchTerm);
     	});
 
     	$(document).on('shown.bs.modal', '#storesModal', function () {
     	    var searchTerm = $('#searchStore input[name="store"]').val();
             $('#searchStore button[type="submit"]').focus();
             loadStores(searchTerm);
         });
 
     	function loadStores(searchTerm) {
     		$('.loader').addClass('show').removeClass('hide');
       		$.get('/stores/store/search/search/'+encodeURIComponent(searchTerm)+'/country_code/de', function(data) {
       			var html 	= $(data).find('#ajaxLoad').html();
       			var lat		= $(data).find('input[name="lat"]').val();
       			var lng		= $(data).find('input[name="lng"]').val();
       			$('input[name="current_position_lat"]').val(lat);
       			$('input[name="current_position_lng"]').val(lng);
       			initialize(lat,lng,'searchResult');
       			$('#storeList').html(html);
       		});
     	}
 
     	$(document).on('click', '.storeLocate', function(event) {
     		initiate_geolocation();
     	});
 
     	function initiate_geolocation() {
             navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(handle_geolocation_query,handle_errors);
         }
 
         function handle_errors(error) {
             switch(error.code) {
                 case error.PERMISSION_DENIED:
                     alert("user did not share geolocation data");
                	    break;
 
                 case error.POSITION_UNAVAILABLE:
                     alert("could not detect current position");
                     break;
 
                 case error.TIMEOUT:
                     alert("retrieving position timed out");
                     break;
 
                 default:
                     alert("unknown error");
                     break;
             }
       	}
 
         function handle_geolocation_query(position) {
     		var lat		= position.coords.latitude;
     		var lng		= position.coords.longitude;
     		$('input[name="current_position_lat"]').val(lat);
     		$('input[name="current_position_lng"]').val(lng);
     		$.get('http://maps.googleapis.com/maps/api/geocode/json?latlng='+lat+','+lng+'&sensor=true', function(data) {
     			if(data.status == 'OK') {
     	  			var results	= data.results;
     	  			if(results[0].formatted_address) {
     					$('input[name="store"]').val(results[0].formatted_address);
     	  			} else {
     	  				$('input[name="store"]').val(lat+','+lng);
     	  			}
     	  		} else {
     	  			$('input[name="store"]').val(lat+','+lng);
     	  		}
     		});
     	}
 
     	function isMobile() {
     		var isMobile = false;
     		if(/(android|bb\d+|meego).+mobile|avantgo|bada\/|blackberry|blazer|compal|elaine|fennec|hiptop|iemobile|ip(hone|od)|ipad|iris|kindle|Android|Silk|lge |maemo|midp|mmp|netfront|opera m(ob|in)i|palm( os)?|phone|p(ixi|re)\/|plucker|pocket|psp|series(4|6)0|symbian|treo|up\.(browser|link)|vodafone|wap|windows (ce|phone)|xda|xiino/i.test(navigator.userAgent)

     		return isMobile;
     	}
     });

     <script type="text/javascript">
      /* <![CDATA[ */
 	jQuery(document).ready(function($){
 		$('.newsletter').on('click', function(){
 			$(this).hide();
 			$('.newsletter-form').show();
 			$('#advancenewsletter-email').focus();
 		});
 		
 		$(document).on('keydown', '#advancenewsletter-dob', function(e){
 	        if ($.inArray(e.keyCode, [46, 8, 9, 27, 13, 110]) !== -1 ||
             (e.keyCode === 65 && (e.ctrlKey === true || e.metaKey === true)) || 
             (e.keyCode >= 35 && e.keyCode <= 40)) {
                  return;
             }
             if ((e.shiftKey || (e.keyCode < 48 || e.keyCode > 57)) && (e.keyCode < 96 || e.keyCode > 105)) {
                 e.preventDefault();
             }
             var currVal = $(this).val();
             var currValLength = currVal.length;
             if (currValLength == 0 && $.inArray(e.keyCode, [48, 49, 50, 51]) == -1){
                e.preventDefault(); 
             }
             if (currValLength == 3 && $.inArray(e.keyCode, [48, 49]) == -1){
                e.preventDefault(); 
             }
             if (currValLength == 1 && currVal.indexOf(3) !== -1 && !(e.keyCode > 47 && e.keyCode < 50)){
                e.preventDefault(); 
             }
             if ( currValLength == 1 && currVal.charAt(0) == 0 && e.keyCode == 48 ){
                 e.preventDefault(); 
             }
             if (currValLength == 4 && currVal.charAt(3) == 1 && !(e.keyCode > 47 && e.keyCode < 51)){
                e.preventDefault(); 
             }else if ( currValLength == 4 && currVal.charAt(3) == 0 && e.keyCode == 48 ){
                e.preventDefault(); 
             }
             if (currValLength == 2){
                 currVal += '.';
                 $(this).val(currVal);
             }
             if (currValLength == 5){
                 currVal += '.';
                 $(this).val(currVal);
             }
             if (currValLength >= 10){
                 e.preventDefault();
                return;
             }
 		});
 		
 		$('.close').on('click', function(){
 			$('.newsletter-form').hide();
 			$('.newsletter').show();
 		});
 		
 		$('.n-box').matchHeight();
 	});
 /* ]]> */
     </script>

 			var homepageblocks_slider = $('#homepageblocks-bottom').bxSlider({
 				controls : false,

 					homepageblocks_slider_initialized = true;
 				},
 				onSliderResize : function() {
 					if (!$(document).isBreakpoint('xs')) {
 						homepageblocks_slider.destroySlider();
 						homepageblocks_slider_initialized = false;
 					}
 				}
 			});
 
 		}
 
 		$(window).resize(function() {
 			if ($(document).isBreakpoint('xs') && !homepageblocks_slider_initialized) {
 
 				var homepageblocks_slider = $('#homepageblocks-bottom').bxSlider({
 					controls : false,
 					onSliderLoad : function() {
 						homepageblocks_slider_initialized = true;
 					},
 					onSliderResize : function() {

     			var magazin_slide_width = thisMagazinSliderContainer.width();
     		}else{
     			var magazin_slide_width = thisMagazinSliderContainer.width() / 3;
     		}
 
 
     		var magazinSlider = $('.magazin-slider').bxSlider({
     			minSlides: $(document).isBreakpoint('xs') ? 1 : 3,
     			maxSlides: 3,
     			slideWidth: magazin_slide_width,
     			slideMargin: 30,
     			adaptiveHeight: true,
     			pager: false,
     			infiniteLoop: false,
     			onSliderLoad  : function(){
     				thisMagazinSliderContainer.find('.bx-controls').appendTo(thisMagazinSliderContainer.find('.product-pager'));
     			},
     			onSliderResize  : function(){
     				resizeTasksMagazin();
     			},
     	  });
 
 
     	  function resizeTasksMagazin (elem){
     		if($(document).isBreakpoint('xs')) {
     			magazinSlider.reloadSlider({
     				minSlides: 1,
     				maxSlides: 1,
     				adaptiveHeight: true,
     				pager: false,
     				slideWidth: 0,
     				slideMargin: 0,
     				infiniteLoop: false,
     				onSliderLoad  : function(){
     					thisMagazinSliderContainer.find('.bx-controls').appendTo(thisMagazinSliderContainer.find('.product-pager'));
     				},
     				onSliderResize  : function(){
     					resizeTasksMagazin();
     				},
     			});
     		}else{
     			magazin_slide_width = thisMagazinSliderContainer.width() / 3;
     			magazinSlider.reloadSlider({
     				minSlides: 3,
     				maxSlides: 3,
     				slideMargin: 30,
     				adaptiveHeight: true,
     				pager: false,
     				infiniteLoop: false,
     				slideWidth: magazin_slide_width,
     				onSliderLoad  : function(){
     					thisMagazinSliderContainer.find('.bx-controls').appendTo(thisMagazinSliderContainer.find('.product-pager'));
     				},
     				onSliderResize  : function(){
     					resizeTasksMagazin();
     				},
     			});
     		}
     	}
 
     });

             <script type="text/javascript">
              var onloadCallback = function() {
             var elements = document.getElementsByClassName('captcha-el');
             for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) { 
                    var thisElem = elements[i];
                    grecaptcha.render(elements[i], {
                     'sitekey': "6Ld3lQwUAAAAANfBw3eiT0DnbKSB7x5Bc2icnTuQ",
                     'theme': "light",
                     'type': "image",
                     'size': "normal",
                     'callback': function(response) {
                         if (response.length > 0) {
                             var form = thisElem.closest('form');
                             var submit = form.querySelector('button[type="submit"]')
                             submit.disabled = false;
                             var checkboxes = document.getElementsByClassName('hidden-check');
                              for (var j = 0; j < checkboxes.length; j++) { 
                                 checkboxes[j].writeAttribute('value', 'checked');
                                 checkboxes[j].checked = true;
                                 
                              }
                         }
                     }
                 });
               elements[i].className  = '';
             }
         };
             </script>
             <script async="" defer="" src="https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api.js?onload=onloadCallback&amp;render=explicit&amp;hl=de">
             </script>

     <script type="text/javascript">
      //<![CDATA[
     var contactForm = new VarienForm('contactForm');
     
     jQuery(document).ready(function($){
         $(document).on('click','#submit-contact-form',function(e){
             e.preventDefault();
             if(contactForm.validator && contactForm.validator.validate()){
                 $(document).loadershow();
                 $.ajax({
                   url: $('#contactForm').attr('action'),
                   data: $('#contactForm').serialize(),
                   method: 'POST',
                 }).done(function(data) {
                   if(data !== ''){
                       var errorArr = jQuery.parseJSON(data);
                       if(errorArr.length > 0){
                         var errorHtml = '<ul class="errors">';
                         $.each(errorArr,function(index){
                             errorHtml += '<li>' + errorArr[index] + '</li>';
                         });
                         errorHtml += '</ul>';
                     
                         $('#modal-contact .modal-messages-block').removeClass('error').html('');
                         $('#modal-contact .modal-messages-block').addClass('error').append(errorHtml);
                       }
                   }else{
                         $('#modal-contact .modal-messages-block').removeClass('error').html('');
                         var html = '<h2 class="text-center">Vielen Dank für Ihre Nachricht!</h2><p class="text-center">Wir werden uns umgehend mit Ihnen in Verbindung setzen</p><button style="margin-top:40px;margin-bottom:40px;" data-dismiss="modal" class="btn button button-red-standard fat center uppercase">Weiter shoppen</button>';
                         $('#modal-contact .modal-body').html(html);
                         $('#modal-contact .modal-header h4').remove();
                   }
                     $(document).loaderclose();
                 });
             }
         });
         $('#modal-contact').on('hidden.bs.modal', function () {
             $(document).loaderclose();
         })
     });
 //]]>
     </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    //<![CDATA[
 jQuery(document).ready(function($){
 
 	$(".rollups .up").on('click',function() {
 		$('html, body').animate({
 			scrollTop: $("#header").offset().top
 		}, 500);
 	});
 
 	$(document).on('click','.e-efficiency',function(){
 
 		console.log('energy');
 
 		var e_sku = $(this).next('.energy_val').html();
 		var e_val = $(this).text().trim();
 
 		var style_black = "position:fixed;height:100%;width:100%;background:#000;opacity:0.6;top:0;left:0;z-index:10000;";
 
 		var blacky = "<div class='blacky' style='" + style_black + "'></div>";
 
 		if (e_val == "A++"){
 			var e_pop = "<div class='epop class-a-plus'><span class='inner'>" + e_sku + "</span></div>";
 		}
 		if (e_val == "C"){
 			var e_pop = "<div class='epop class-c'><span class='inner'>" + e_sku + "</span></div>";
 		}
 		if (e_val == "A"){
 			var e_pop = "<div class='epop class-a'><span class='inner'>" + e_sku + "</span></div>";
 		}
 
 		$('body').append(blacky);
 		$('body').append(e_pop);
 	});
 
 	$(document).on('click','.blacky , .epop',function(){
 		$('.epop').remove();
 		$('.blacky').remove();
 	});
 
 	$('img').unveil();
 
 });
 //]]>
   </script>
